line=11538 tag=M:       Narrator: Huang Chenglong
line=11539 tag=M:       Born 1968
line=11540 tag=M:       Recorded 1994
line=11541 tag=B:
line=11542 tag=B:
line=11543 tag=B:
line=11544 tag=T:                                The Creation of the World
line=11545 tag=B:
line=11546 tag=T:       Long, long ago, there were nine suns in the heaven which burned the
line=11547 tag=T:       earth. Because a brother and younger sister hid in a great cypress (that
line=11548 tag=T:       honored the gods), they were not burned to death. Later, in order to
line=11549 tag=T:       propagate descendants, the brother and sister talked it over and decided
line=11550 tag=T:       that each would carry a stone mill on his or her back and roll it down
line=11551 tag=T:       from the mountain peak. If the two stone mills joined together, the two
line=11552 tag=T:       could get married. As it happened, when the two stone mills rolled
line=11553 tag=T:       down (to the river bank) they joined together, and so the brother and
line=11554 tag=T:       sister married. After a few years, the younger sister gave birth to a
line=11555 tag=T:       monster not of human form. The older brother was so angry he used a
line=11556 tag=T:       curved knife/scythe to chop it into pieces and scattered them wildly
line=11557 tag=T:       everywhere. The next day when they got up, they saw the smoke of
line=11558 tag=T:       cooking fires everywhere. And henceforth there was humankind.

line=11695 tag=M:       Narrator: Huang Chenglong
line=11696 tag=M:       Born 1968
line=11697 tag=M:       Recorded 1994

line=11699 tag=B:
line=11700 tag=B:
line=11701 tag=M:                       The Legend of the Origin of All Things
line=11702 tag=M:                                 t it              t
line=11703 tag=M:                              Muttsiitt®u and Tugantt®u
line=11704 tag=B:
line=11705 tag=T:          (The goddess) Mutsit®u and (the mortal man) Tugant®u wanted to
line=11706 tag=T:       come down to the earth. The god Mupitha said to them, ÆÆIf you want to
line=11707 tag=T:       go down to the earth, then go.flfl Just before Mutsit®u and Tugant®u left,
line=11708 tag=T:       Mupitha gave them three bushels of China fir seeds and instructed them
line=11709 tag=T:       to plant them on low mountains. He also gave them three bushels of
line=11710 tag=T:       seeds for thorned bushes, and instructed them to plant them on high
line=11711 tag=T:       mountains. He also gave them a hundred kinds of livestock, which they
line=11712 tag=T:       drove before them, and a thousand kinds of birds and beasts, which
line=11713 tag=T:       followed behind them. When they parted, Mupitha said to them, ÆÆWhen
line=11714 tag=T:       you are on the road, do not look back at heaven.flfl
line=11715 tag=T:          Mutsit®u and Tugant®u were extremely happy. The whole way they
line=11716 tag=T:       sang and danced as they walked. Because the god Mupitha had opposed
line=11717 tag=T:       them becoming one family before, they deliberately looked back at
line=11718 tag=T:       heaven, and the result was that they frightened the thousand kinds of
line=11719 tag=T:       birds and beasts following them, causing them to flee everywhere. In
line=11720 tag=T:       this way these animals became the wild animals now dwelling in the
line=11721 tag=T:       forests. After Mutsit®u and Tugant®u arrived on the earth, they
line=11722 tag=T:       misremembered (what Mupitha had told them to do) and sowed the
line=11723 tag=T:       China fir seeds on high mountains and the thorny bushes on low
line=11724 tag=T:       mountains. As a result, the low areas grew full of brambles and thorns.
line=11725 tag=T:       (However,) because they were very able, they cut down the China firs
line=11726 tag=T:       and built houses, and they hacked through the brambles and thorns,
line=11727 tag=T:       opening up wilderness land, and planted the grain needed by
line=11728 tag=T:       humankind.

line=12449 tag=B:
line=12450 tag=T:                                        An Orphan
line=12451 tag=B:
line=12452 tag=T:           Long ago, there was an orphan; he was one who had no father         and
line=12453 tag=T:        no mother. There was an orangutan who wanted to eat this orphan.       The
line=12454 tag=T:        orphan was always afraid when it got dark at night, and on his         way
line=12455 tag=T:        home, he was crying and crying as he walked. He walked a while         and
line=12456 tag=T:        met with a needle. The needle asked him, ÆÆWhatfls the matter?flfl     The
line=12457 tag=B:
line=12458 tag=M:                                                            Text 3: An Orphan    267
line=12459 tag=B:
line=12460 tag=B:
line=12461 tag=T:  orphan answered, ÆÆAye! The orangutan is going to come eat me at
line=12462 tag=T:  night. Iflm afraid to be at home by myself.flfl The needle said, ÆÆHah!
line=12463 tag=T:  Donflt be afraid. At night Iflll come be your companion.flfl
line=12464 tag=T:      Later, again he was crying, crying as he walked. He walked a while
line=12465 tag=T:  and met some scissors. The scissors asked him, ÆÆAh, whatfls the matter
line=12466 tag=T:  with you? Why are you crying like this?flfl The orphan said, ÆÆAt my
line=12467 tag=T:  home, therefls only me alone. The orangutan is going to come down to
line=12468 tag=T:  eat me. He comes at night.flfl The scissors said, ÆÆAh, if that is all it is, no
line=12469 tag=T:  problem, at night Iflll come be your companion.flfl
line=12470 tag=T:      After that, the orphan still was crying and crying as he walked. He
line=12471 tag=T:  walked a while and met a magpie. The magpie asked him, ÆÆWhy are
line=12472 tag=T:  you crying like this?flfl The orphan answered, ÆÆAt home, therefls only me
line=12473 tag=T:  alone. I have neither father nor mother. I am one without parents. When
line=12474 tag=T:  it gets dark, the orangutan is going to eat me. Iflm afraid to be at home
line=12475 tag=T:  alone.flfl The magpie said, ÆÆAye! You need not be afraid. At night Iflll
line=12476 tag=T:  come be your companion.flfl
line=12477 tag=T:      Again he went on, and after walking a while he met a crow, and the
line=12478 tag=T:  crow said, ÆÆHah! Why are you crying?flfl The orphan said, ÆÆI have
line=12479 tag=T:  neither father nor mother. Iflm only an orphan. At night I am afraid (to
line=12480 tag=T:  be at home alone); the orangutan is going to eat me.flfl The crow said,
line=12481 tag=T:  ÆÆHah! If thatfls the case, therefls no problem, at night Iflll come be your
line=12482 tag=T:  companion.flfl
line=12483 tag=T:      Again, the orphan went on crying as he walked. He walked a while
line=12484 tag=T:  and came across a stomach, and the stomach asked him, ÆÆHah! Why are
line=12485 tag=T:  you crying like this?flfl The orphan answered, ÆÆI have neither father nor
line=12486 tag=T:  mother. At night, as soon as it gets dark, the orangutan is going to come
line=12487 tag=T:  eat me. Iflm afraid.flfl The stomach said, ÆÆHah! If thatfls all it is, therefls no
line=12488 tag=T:  problem, let me come be your companion at night. Iflll come be your
line=12489 tag=T:  companion.flfl
line=12490 tag=T:      The orphan still was crying, crying as he walked. He walked a while
line=12491 tag=T:  and also came across a stone mortar, the stone mortar asked, ÆÆHah!
line=12492 tag=T:  Why are you crying like this?flfl The orphan said, ÆÆAh, I have neither
line=12493 tag=T:  father nor mother. Iflm afraid of when it will get dark. When it gets dark
line=12494 tag=T:  again today, the orangutan is going to come eat me.flfl The stone mortar
line=12495 tag=T:  said, ÆÆIf thatfls all it is, no problem, Iflll come be your companion. Let
line=12496 tag=T:  me come be your companion.flfl
line=12497 tag=T:      At this time the orphan had made friends with these (things)
line=12498 tag=T:  mentioned. When night came, they all came. The needle came, and the
line=12499 tag=T:  scissors came, and the magpie came, and the crow came, and the
line=12500 tag=T:  stomach, the stone mortar and a stone pestle all came. After they came,
line=12501 tag=T:  they held a meeting. The orphan was extremely happy. ÆÆTonight my
line=12502 tag=T:  companions have come. Tonight Iflm not afraid of the orangutan.flfl After
line=12503 tag=T:  these [things] had all come, they told him, ÆÆDonflt be afraid tonight. If
line=12504 tag=T:  the orangutan comes, we will beat him to death.flfl
line=12505 tag=B:
line=12506 tag=M:        Texts
line=12507 tag=B:  268
line=12508 tag=B:
line=12509 tag=B:
line=12510 tag=T:       The orangutan wasnflt afraid, and still came. The orphan was not
line=12511 tag=T:  afraid.
line=12512 tag=T:       That night everybody made a plan together, where the needle should
line=12513 tag=T:  stay, where (each of them) should sleep and what-not and it was all
line=12514 tag=T:  settled. The needle was above the door to stab (the orangutan) in the
line=12515 tag=T:  doorway, the scissors slept beside the orphan on the bed, the magpie
line=12516 tag=T:  slept in the fire pile, the crow slept in the water jar, the stomach slept at
line=12517 tag=T:  the head of the stairs, the stone mortar was at the foot of the stairs, and
line=12518 tag=T:  the stone pestle was at the head of the stairs.
line=12519 tag=T:       When it got dark, the orangutan came towards the orphan, the same
line=12520 tag=T:  as before. When he pushed the door with a creak, the needle was there,
line=12521 tag=T:  and as soon as the needle pricked his hand, his hand was all covered
line=12522 tag=T:  with blood, but he still wanted to go in the room. Once he was in the
line=12523 tag=T:  room and going to look for the orphan in the bed, the scissors cut off his
line=12524 tag=T:  hand. It was dark and the scissors had cut off his hand, and blood was
line=12525 tag=T:  dripping down. Then he went over to the fire pile, thinking to light it, to
line=12526 tag=T:  see what thing it was! As soon as the orangutan wanted to touch the fire
line=12527 tag=T:  pile, the magpie inside the fire pile burst out with a lot of noise and (the
line=12528 tag=T:  ashes) got into the orangutanfls eyes. The orangutan went to the water
line=12529 tag=T:  jar, wanting to get some water to wash his face. He looked around and
line=12530 tag=T:  saw the water jar and after a mouthful of water wanted to wash his face,
line=12531 tag=T:  but the crow was there and the crow came out and pecked his eyes. This
line=12532 tag=T:  time the orangutan had no eyes and no hand and was covered with
line=12533 tag=T:  blood. He wanted to escape covered with blood. As soon as he got to
line=12534 tag=T:  the head of the stairs he stepped on the stomach and slipped and rolled
line=12535 tag=T:  down the staircase and into the stone mortar at the foot of the stairs.
line=12536 tag=T:  Then the stone pestle pounded and pounded and pounded down on him,
line=12537 tag=T:  and in this way pounded the orangutan to death and then (they) threw
line=12538 tag=T:  him away.

line=12825 tag=T:                                       Uncle Snake
line=12826 tag=B:
line=12827 tag=T:           Look, today the Snake (Uncle) is bringing ramfls horn flowers.108
line=12828 tag=T:       He says (to the father), ÆÆIf you donflt give one of your daughters to me, I
line=12829 tag=T:       will chop off your hand.flfl After Snake (Uncle) said this, the youngest
line=12830 tag=T:       daughter said (to her father), ÆÆPapa, itfls better I do what I have to do
line=12831 tag=T:       and go become his (Snake's) wife, than for your hand to be cut off.flfl
line=12832 tag=T:           (The girlfls family) gave her a basketful of momo (a kind of bread)
line=12833 tag=T:       (and said to her), ÆÆYou go with Uncle Snake then.flfl Uncle Snake went
line=12834 tag=T:       in front of the girl. The girl carried the momo and was crying and crying
line=12835 tag=T:       as she followed behind Uncle Snake. They kept going until they came
line=12836 tag=T:       to a pile of rocks, and then Uncle Snake disappeared. He had gone into
line=12837 tag=T:       the pile through a crevice in the rocks. The girl continued to cry in the
line=12838 tag=T:       courtyard beside the pile of rocks.
line=12839 tag=T:           In fact, Uncle Snake was a god and he sent a chicken to call the girl.
line=12840 tag=T:       The chicken called, ÆÆAunt-in-lawflfl three times, but the girl didnflt
line=12841 tag=T:       understand and still cried there.
line=12842 tag=T:           Later, the chicken went in and a dog was sent out to call the girl to
line=12843 tag=T:       come inside. The dog also barked two times, but the girl still didnflt
line=12844 tag=T:       understand, and still cried there.
line=12845 tag=T:           In like manner a pig was sent to call her, and the girl still didnflt
line=12846 tag=T:       understand and so didnflt enter.
line=12847 tag=B:
line=12848 tag=M:        Texts
line=12849 tag=B:  274
line=12850 tag=B:
line=12851 tag=B:
line=12852 tag=T:      Finally, an old woman came out to call her (Snakefls mother came
line=12853 tag=T:  out to call her), and said to the girl, ÆÆChild, what are you crying about?
line=12854 tag=T:  Donflt cry. Iflve sent many to call you, but you havenflt come in, so I
line=12855 tag=T:  came out myself.flfl The girl said, ÆÆI didnflt understand.flfl The old mother-
line=12856 tag=T:  in-law said, ÆÆIf you didnflt understand, close your eyes and hold on to
line=12857 tag=T:  my clothes, and come with me.flfl When they went in, she gave the girl
line=12858 tag=T:  something (skupu), and she went back inside. Inside it was as if a
line=12859 tag=T:  wedding was being held, and Uncle Snake and others were drinking
line=12860 tag=T:  wine. In this way, the girl became Uncle Snakefls wife.

line=14322 tag=T:                                The Story of a Lazy Man
line=14323 tag=B:
line=14324 tag=T:            A long time ago there were two sisters. The husband of the older
line=14325 tag=T:        sister was the emperor (previously called /juånÙuåi/, now called
line=14326 tag=T:        /Âmt®i/). The younger sister had a son who was very lazy. Every day
line=14327 tag=T:        the mother would weigh out half a catty of wool and spin yarn. The son
line=14328 tag=T:        liked to drink liquor and often went to a restaurant in town to drink.
line=14329 tag=T:        When he returned, he often brought back half a catty of liquor for his
line=14330 tag=T:        mother.
line=14331 tag=T:            One day the older sister went to her younger sisterfls home and
line=14332 tag=T:        chatted with her. The younger sister told the older one, ÆÆMy son is very
line=14333 tag=T:        lazy.flfl One day the younger sisterfls son pretended to go to town but hid
line=14334 tag=T:        behind the door. The older and younger sister chatted inside and the son
line=14335 tag=T:        of the younger sister listened from behind the door. The two sisters
line=14336 tag=T:        spoke of the younger sisterfls son. This son had not gone to town, but
line=14337 tag=T:        was behind the door secretly listening. They said things like ÆÆMy son is
line=14338 tag=T:        very lazy.flfl
line=14339 tag=T:            The younger sisterfls son then said to his mother, ÆÆIflm back. Today I
line=14340 tag=T:        learned an ability.flfl The younger sister asked, ÆÆSon, what ability did
line=14341 tag=T:        you learn?flfl The son said, ÆÆWhat were you saying today at home?
line=14342 tag=T:        When I was in the restaurant in the center of town, I heard what you
line=14343 tag=T:        said (what you said, I learned to be able to hear it all).flfl The two sisters
line=14344 tag=T:        said, ÆÆWhat did we say?flfl The son of the younger sister said, ÆÆWhen I
line=14345 tag=T:        was in the restaurant in town, I heard you say this and that.flfl The
line=14346 tag=T:        younger sister said, ÆÆThatfls really how it was, son.flfl
line=14347 tag=B:
line=14348 tag=M:                                           Text 5: The Story of a Lazy Man   297
line=14349 tag=B:
line=14350 tag=B:
line=14351 tag=T:      The older sisterfls husband was emperor. The younger sister then
line=14352 tag=T:  said, ÆÆIf my son has learned this kind of ability, it really is a good
line=14353 tag=T:  thing.flfl One day, the older sisterfls husband was preparing for his
line=14354 tag=T:  birthday. He bought three yak and tethered them inside a cowpen. The
line=14355 tag=T:  son of the younger sister, the one who said ÆÆI have learned an abilityflfl,
line=14356 tag=T:  at night stole the yaks and crossed the mountain and tethered them in a
line=14357 tag=T:  mountain cave. The emperor could not proceed with his birthday
line=14358 tag=T:  (celebration). The older sister said to her husband (the emperor), ÆÆMy
line=14359 tag=T:  younger sisterfls son has an ability. He can see in his dreams where
line=14360 tag=T:  something is. When he listens, he can hear.flfl This emperor had soldiers,
line=14361 tag=T:  and sent his soldiers to look for the lost yaks. After this person had
line=14362 tag=T:  stolen the yaks, he tied them in a cave on the mountain. He himself
line=14363 tag=T:  knew, and he was relaxed and carefree. Almost at the river
line=14364 tag=T:  embankment, the person searching said, a little faster. See if itfls
line=14365 tag=T:  possible to find [the yaks] a day or two ahead of time. [The one with an
line=14366 tag=T:  ability] brought a bamboo tube, and he himself asked on the bamboo
line=14367 tag=T:  tube and he himself answered (he asked himself and answered himself).
line=14368 tag=T:  One day, the older sisterfls husband (formerly called /juånÙuåi/
line=14369 tag=T:  [emperor], now called /Âmt®i/ [emperor]) said, ÆÆIf one is able to go
line=14370 tag=T:  faster, then go a little faster. Those who can go tomorrow and can go
line=14371 tag=T:  fast must all go search.flfl In this manner he selected a propitious day,
line=14372 tag=T:  and after the propitious day was selected, notified people everywhere.
line=14373 tag=T:  ÆÆThose who can go, and who can hear all come here. We will hold a
line=14374 tag=T:  meeting, and all must come here.flfl On a cart this person [with an
line=14375 tag=T:  ability] used the bamboo tube to ask [the whereabouts of the yaks] on
line=14376 tag=T:  the day the meeting was held. On the cart he used the bamboo tube to
line=14377 tag=T:  ask where the emperorfls livestock had been lost. There he said, ÆÆAfter a
line=14378 tag=T:  thief took the livestock, he drove them up on the mountain and tethered
line=14379 tag=T:  them in a mountain cave. Quickly now go over that mountain.flfl
line=14380 tag=T:  Through the bamboo tube he himself answered and he himself asked.
line=14381 tag=T:  After asking, he said, ÆÆYou see, that thief stole them. Quickly cross
line=14382 tag=T:  over that mountain. They are there!flfl This child of the older sisterfls
line=14383 tag=T:  family, this familyfls soldiers and the other people went to look, and
line=14384 tag=T:  when they went to look, the livestock really was there. At this time, as
line=14385 tag=T:  for this person, well! The younger sisterfls sonfls reputation went up
line=14386 tag=T:  greatly. Whatever the older sisterfls husband ate, he ate; whatever the
line=14387 tag=T:  emperor drank, he drank. It was discussed and agreed in advance to
line=14388 tag=T:  provide for him this way. Thus, this personfls problems were solved.
line=14389 tag=B:
line=14390 tag=B:
line=14391 tag=B:  ---
line=14392 tag=T:      Later, that time, the emperor of another place lost a ÆÆdzinflfl (also
line=14393 tag=T:  called a ÆÆjin.flfl A monkfls robe or ÆÆHuang Ma Guaflfl). After the emperor
line=14394 tag=T:  had lost the dzin, he was chatting with another person and learned about
line=14395 tag=B:
line=14396 tag=M:        Texts
line=14397 tag=B:  298
line=14398 tag=B:
line=14399 tag=B:
line=14400 tag=T:  (it). The emperor said, ÆÆ(I) must have this person go search. This person
line=14401 tag=T:  can dream or hear otherfls words. This person has much ability.flfl A
line=14402 tag=T:  person of this family took a message to him, and after taking him the
line=14403 tag=T:  message, he will find the emperorfls dzin. After this person finds the
line=14404 tag=T:  dzin, the emperor will provide for him. He set a time, he set a time of
line=14405 tag=T:  seven days. ÆÆWithin seven days he must find the emperorfls dzin in his
line=14406 tag=T:  dreams. The difficulty is great.flfl
line=14407 tag=T:       For seven days and seven nights this person ate and drank at the
line=14408 tag=T:  emperor's. After eating, one day, the emperor said to him, ÆÆAi! My dzin
line=14409 tag=T:  has been moved somewhere by someone.flfl One day, the son ate too
line=14410 tag=T:  much and went to the toilet to relieve himself. There was a cat which
line=14411 tag=T:  had moved some roof tiles on top of the toilet and hidden the emperorfls
line=14412 tag=T:  dzin among the tiles. When he went to look, he discovered the
line=14413 tag=T:  emperorfls dzin. He said, ÆÆThis brindled cat has done me a good deed,flfl
line=14414 tag=T:  and took the dzin from the cat. He counted seven tiles, and stood up
line=14415 tag=T:  seven rows vertically; he hid the emperorfls dzin there. At this time, the
line=14416 tag=T:  emperor said, ÆÆit will be a little difficult for you to find the dzin. I am
line=14417 tag=T:  willing to move to another place. How about that?flfl That person then
line=14418 tag=T:  said, ÆÆYou come tomorrowflfl (we say ÆÆsoqhuiflfl [tomorrow], and it can
line=14419 tag=T:  also be said ÆÆtpiflfl [tomorrow]). ÆÆTonight Iflll try to divine [its
line=14420 tag=T:  whereabouts], all right? Tomorrow Iflll notify you and notify those who
line=14421 tag=T:  can walk and who can hear to come. These people must all come.flfl To
line=14422 tag=T:  organize a meeting, this is how he spoke to the emperor. The next day, a
line=14423 tag=T:  meeting was held. He used the bamboo tube and asked himself and
line=14424 tag=T:  answered himself, where is the dzin. This person had them go look,
line=14425 tag=T:  counting out which roof tile in which row of tiles on which toilet. The
line=14426 tag=T:  emperorfls dzin was in fact there. After finding it, they notified the
line=14427 tag=T:  emperor, and the emperor said to him, ÆÆWhatever I eat, you eat; when I
line=14428 tag=T:  sit, you sit; when I stand, you stand.flfl In the end, he was even better
line=14429 tag=T:  provided for.
line=14430 tag=B:
line=14431 tag=B:
line=14432 tag=B:  --
line=14433 tag=T:       There was another emperor who lost (had stolen) a very expensive
line=14434 tag=T:  kind of parrot, perhaps for revenge. After losing it, this emperor who
line=14435 tag=T:  had lost the dzin told this person who had lost the parrot, ÆÆA dog barks
line=14436 tag=T:  in that direction. You have lost this kind of bird, and I have there (in my
line=14437 tag=T:  place) one of this kind of bird.flfl A person came here to search. When he
line=14438 tag=T:  went to search, those people set a time to feed this parrot. ÆÆThis parrot
line=14439 tag=T:  of mine isnflt a dead treasure, itfls a living treasure. It might starve to
line=14440 tag=T:  death someplace. If you can dream of it a little faster, see or hear it, do
line=14441 tag=T:  it a little faster for me. If you can find the parrot, you may rise and sit
line=14442 tag=T:  with me (as my equal) and like me eat what I eat, stand when I stand, sit
line=14443 tag=T:  when I sit.flfl The day he went to look for the parrot, he went to a place
line=14444 tag=B:
line=14445 tag=M:                                            Text 5: The Story of a Lazy Man   299
line=14446 tag=B:
line=14447 tag=B:
line=14448 tag=T:  where Han people live and went to relieve himself. Where the Han
line=14449 tag=T:  people live, each family grew bamboo. By the roadside there was row
line=14450 tag=T:  after row of bamboo trees. There was a rope tied around a small stick
line=14451 tag=T:  attached to the parrotfls wing. The rope was wedged in the bamboo
line=14452 tag=T:  forest. This person couldnflt find a toilet, so he went to relieve himself
line=14453 tag=T:  beside the bamboo forest. While relieving himself, he heard the parrot
line=14454 tag=T:  calling in the bamboo forest. He said, ÆÆThis parrot has done a good
line=14455 tag=T:  thing for me,flfl and he caught the parrot. After catching it, he counted
line=14456 tag=T:  the rows of bamboo and put the parrot there. The emperor said, ÆÆMy
line=14457 tag=T:  living treasure might starve to death (it would be a disaster). Itfls a living
line=14458 tag=T:  treasure which may die someplace. If it could eat a little something as
line=14459 tag=T:  soon as possible, then like me, what I eat, you will eat.flfl After this, they
line=14460 tag=T:  set a time (came to an agreement on it), and this person brought up the
line=14461 tag=T:  bamboo tube. He used the tube to eat (earn his living). Perhaps he had
line=14462 tag=T:  this kind of luck. This person was called Huang Qianmen. Huang
line=14463 tag=T:  Qianmen brought the parrot back and said to the emperor, ÆÆYou must
line=14464 tag=T:  give me three things. These three things you must proclaim to the
line=14465 tag=T:  people.flfl In the end, Huang Qianmen lived just like the emperor.
line=14466 tag=B:
line=14467 tag=B:
line=14468 tag=B:  --
line=14469 tag=T:      This emperor said, ÆÆThe person who finds the parrot will marry my
line=14470 tag=T:  daughter and sit on my throne. (The Huang Qianmen I spoke of is the
line=14471 tag=T:  person I called ÆÆthis personflfl before. When I was talking before, I forgot
line=14472 tag=T:  his name. This personfls name is Huang Qianmen.) The emperor said,
line=14473 tag=T:  ÆÆTo the person who finds the parrot I will marry my daughter,flfl so
line=14474 tag=T:  Huang Qianmen married his daughter and became emperor.

line=16160 tag=M:        Narrator: Yu Zelong
line=16161 tag=M:        Born 1960
line=16162 tag=M:        Recorded 1996
line=16163 tag=B:
line=16164 tag=B:
line=16165 tag=B:
line=16166 tag=T:                            The Old Man of the Chen Family
line=16167 tag=B:
line=16168 tag=T:             Long ago there was an old man named Chen and another person.
line=16169 tag=T:        Every day they went hunting. They made a living hunting. One day they
line=16170 tag=T:        went up the mountain to hunt but didnflt get a single animal. In a
line=16171 tag=T:        mountain cave they saw a snake and said, ÆÆToday we didnflt get
line=16172 tag=T:        anything. It looks like weflll have to return empty-handed. Itfls better to
line=16173 tag=T:        kill [this snake] weflve just seen with one shot.flfl After they shot it once,
line=16174 tag=T:        [it turned out that] this wasnflt a snake at all, but was an evil demon that
line=16175 tag=T:        ate people. He strangled it to death. She was the wife of the emperor
line=16176 tag=T:        (today we say /Âmt®i/, before we said /juånÙuai/ for Æemperorfl), and
line=16177 tag=T:        had changed into an evil demon who ate people. ... The emperor said
line=16178 tag=T:        ÆÆGo find herflfl, and sent people to find her. (After they found her) this
line=16179 tag=T:        evil demon who ate people pretended to be sick. The emperor asked,
line=16180 tag=T:        ÆÆWhat illness do you have? The doctor canflt cure it. What will you
line=16181 tag=T:        do?flfl The evil demon who ate people answered, ÆÆIf I eat the kidney and
line=16182 tag=T:        heart of Old Man Chen, I can be cured.flfl
line=16183 tag=T:             The emperor sent soldiers to find Old Man Chen. Old Man Chenfls
line=16184 tag=T:        son was called Chen Diqing. Old Man Chen could foretell peoplefls
line=16185 tag=T:        future. He divined his own future and said to his son Chen Diqing,
line=16186 tag=T:        ÆÆThey are looking for me, son. Hurry and leave. I cannot escape.
line=16187 tag=T:        Because that day in the mountain cave I saw a snake, this snake (evil
